--- Commit Message ---
LU-10026 osd-ldiskfs: use preallocation for dense writes

use inode's preallocation chunks as per-inode group preallocation:
just grab the very first available blocks from the window.

Patch Set 15:

> Andreas, don't you think we should introduce sanity-csdc instead of
 > adding more tests to sanity?

Yes, I do.  Having a simple compression test in sanity is still a good idea, but the majority should go into a new sanity-compr.sh that runs all of sanity and sanityn with a default compressed layout, like sanity-dom.sh to get better usage coverage.  See EX-5771 for my comments on this.
